#SV1
select max(s.submission_id) from submission s join zip_submission_result zr on s.submission_id = zr.submission_id where s.student_id =  1 and s.course_problem_id = 17 and s.runtime_result_id != 9  and zr.junit_score > 0 group by s.total_score order by  s.total_score desc, s.created_at desc
INTO OUTFILE '/var/lib/mysql-files/problem_7_student_1.txt'
FIELDS TERMINATED BY ';'
LINES TERMINATED BY ';';
